However, if she was devoid of regular emotions, she would not be able to feel pleasure, so (A) can be eliminated. This leaves us with (D) and (E). If she was devoid of regular emotions, she would not be able to feel owning something, so (E) can be eliminated. This leaves us with (D) as the answer. 
Therefore, among A through E, the answer is D.
